***toestand.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toestand.html>toestand</a> (2143)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:toestand.html>toestand</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">toestaen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to assist</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toestaan.html>toestaan</a></i>) and <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stand</i> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">stand</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toestand.html>toestand</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toestanden.html>toestanden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toestand.html>toestandje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>situation, condition</li>
<li>an unpleasant situation</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">physics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> state
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:aangeslagen.html>aangeslagen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toestand.html>toestand</a></i>  |  excited state</dd>
<dd><i>grondtoestand</i>  |  ground state</dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:toestand.html>toestand</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>

***toestemmen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toestemmen.html>toestemmen</a> (34622)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toe.html>toe</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to(<a href = vnd.unilang:wards.html>wards</a>)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stemmen.html>stemmen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to speak</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, perfectly parallel to the cognate German equivalent <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">zustimmen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toestemmen.html>toestemmen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To consent, agree</li>
<li>(<i>unusual</i>) <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To award</li>
<li>(<i>unusual</i>) <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To allow</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To admit, acknowledge</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">accident</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">chance</span>
<dl><dd><i>In september 1928 <a href = vnd.unilang:ontdekte.html>ontdekte</a> Fleming <a href = vnd.unilang:eigenlijk.html>eigenlijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toeval.html>toeval</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:buurt.html>buurt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bepaalde.html>bepaalde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schimmel.html>schimmel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> per <a href = vnd.unilang:ongeluk.html>ongeluk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> bacteriekoloniën <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gekomen.html>gekomen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bacterie.html>bacteriën</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:groeiden.html>groeiden</a>.</i><sup><a class="external autonumber" href="https://nl.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alexander_Fleming">[1]</a></sup>  |  In September 1928 Fleming discovered, actually by <a href = vnd.unilang:serendipity.html>serendipity</a>, that in the neighborhood of a certain fungus that through bad luck <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> come into one of his bacteria colonies, no bacteria grew.</dd></dl></li>
<li>an <span class="Latn" lang="en">attack</span> (of <span class="Latn" lang="en">epilepsy</span>)</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toga.html>toga</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toga.html>toga</a>'s</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toga.html>togaatje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:toga.html>toga</a></span>, an outer garment worn by Roman patrician <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a>.</li>
<li>A gown worn by academics, Christian priests or ministers, and certain members of the legal profession.</li></ol>

</p>

<p>A frequentive verb derived from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">tokken</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-elen</i> (to pull, tap, tick).

***toko.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toko.html>toko</a> (24027)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From Indonesian <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malay_language" class="extiw" title="w:Malay language">Malay</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ms"><a href = vnd.unilang:toko.html>toko</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shop</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Southern_Min" class="extiw" title="w:Southern Min"><a href = vnd.unilang:min.html>Min</a> Nan</a></span> <span class="Hani" lang="zh">土庫</span>／<span class="Hani" lang="zh">土库</span> (<i><span class="tr Latn">thó͘-khò͘</span></i>, “private storehouse”).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toko.html>toko</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toko.html>toko</a>'s</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toko.html>tokootje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> referring to Indonesia</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a Dutch, otherwise European or Chinese shop <span class="defdate">[19th to 20th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1879</b> May 26, W. F. <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Erp, "<a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toko.html>toko</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:keurig.html>keurige</a> provisien." (advertisement), <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:locomotief.html>locomotief</a>. Samarangsch handels- <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> advertentie-blad</i>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>vol</a>. 28, issue 120, page 4.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toko.html>Toko</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> puike <a href = vnd.unilang:dranken.html>Dranken</a>.<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toko.html>Toko</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fraaie.html>fraaie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:cadeautjes.html>Cadeautjes</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> koopen<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toko.html>Toko</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sterke.html>sterke</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:mooie.html>mooie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ijzeren.html>Ijzeren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ledikant.html>Ledikanten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> toebehooren <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> koopen.<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toko.html>Toko</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alle.html>alle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:soorten.html>soorten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:banket.html>Banket</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> SUIKERWERK. <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">A <b>shop</b> for excellent DRINKS.<br />A <b>shop</b> where you can buy beautiful GIFTS<br />A <b>shop</b> where you can buy strong, beautiful IRON COTS with accessories.<br />A <b>shop</b> for all <a href = vnd.unilang:types.html>types</a> of BANQUET and <a href = vnd.unilang:sweets.html>Sweets</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:told.html>told</a> (98655)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:tolde.html>tolde</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">talde</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">first and third person singular preterite</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">tealde</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">first and third person singular preterite</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*talid-</i>, preterite <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a> of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*taljaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to count; tell</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tell</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-ed</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:told.html>told</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">simple past tense and past participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tell</i></span></span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">A tale <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> but <a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:told.html>told</a></b>, if only one person <a href = vnd.unilang:tells.html>tells</a> it.</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tollenâer</i>. ***tom.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tom.html>tom</a> (938)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From generic use of the proper name <i><a href = vnd.unilang:tom.html>Tom</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tom.html>tom</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:toms.html>toms</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The male of the domesticated cat.</li>
<li>The male of the turkey.</li>
<li>The male of the orangutan.</li>
<li>The male of certain other animals.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> prostitutes</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A lesbian.</li>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The <a href = vnd.unilang:jack.html>jack</a> of trumps in the card game gleek.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> regional<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A close-stool.</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:cockney.html>Cockney</a> rhyming <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> jewellery</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tomatenplant.html>tomatenplant</a> (78920)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tomaat.html>tomaat</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">plant</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tombola.html>tombola</a> (53022)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:tombola.html>tombola</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tombola.html>tombola</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tombolas</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A lottery in which winning <a href = vnd.unilang:tickets.html>tickets</a> are drawn from a revolving drum.
<ul><li><b>1991</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stephen_Fry" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Stephen Fry">Stephen Fry</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Liar_(novel)" class="extiw" title="w:The Liar (novel)">The Liar</a></i>, p. 60:
<dl><dd>He <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> given no choice in the matter of sharing <a href = vnd.unilang:rooms.html>rooms</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:gary.html>Gary</a> and he <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> drawn out of the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tombola.html>tombola</a></b> together, so together they <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:tombola.html>tombola</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span> <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>

***tombstone.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tombstone.html>tombstone</a> (24366)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tomb</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">stone</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tombstone.html>tombstone</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tombstones</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A headstone marking a person's grave.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">headstone</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">gravestone</span></span></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1922</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Virginia_Woolf" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Virginia Woolf">Virginia Woolf</a>,  chapter 2, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jacob%27s_Room" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Jacob | s Room"><a href = vnd.unilang:jacob.html>Jacob</a>'s Room</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">True, there's no harm in <a href = vnd.unilang:crying.html>crying</a> for one's husband, and the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tombstone.html>tombstone</a></b>, though plain, <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a solid piece of work, and on summer's days when the widow <a href = vnd.unilang:brought.html>brought</a> her boys to stand there one felt kindly towards her.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The symbol "<i class="Zmth mention" lang="mul">∎</i>" marking the end of a proof.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">halmos</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing<span class="ib-comma">,</span> Microsoft <a href = vnd.unilang:windows.html>Windows</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A marker that <a href = vnd.unilang:takes.html>takes</a> the place of deleted data, allowing for replication of the deletion across <a href = vnd.unilang:servers.html>servers</a> etc.
<ul><li><b>2008</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:laura.html>Laura</a> E. Hunter, ‎Robbie <a href = vnd.unilang:allen.html>Allen</a>, <i>Active Directory Cookbook</i> (page 739)
<dl><dd>If you attempt to restore a backup that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> older than the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tombstone.html>tombstone</a></b> lifetime, it may introduce <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a> that <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> deleted <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A crashdump.
<ul><li><b>2014</b>, Joshua J. <a href = vnd.unilang:drake.html>Drake</a>, ‎Zach <a href = vnd.unilang:lanier.html>Lanier</a>, ‎Collin Mulliner, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:android.html>Android</a> Hacker's Handbook</i> (page 186)
<dl><dd>This actually results in a crash dump, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> written to the log and to a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tombstone.html>tombstone</a></b> file.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">cardiology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An unusual morphological feature on an electrocardiogram indicative of acute myocardial infarction, characterized by a massive ST elevation.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tombstone.html>tombstone</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">tombstones</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tombstoning</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tombstoned</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To take part in tombstoning: to jump into the sea, etc. from a <a href = vnd.unilang:cliff.html>cliff</a> or other high point so as to enter the water vertically straight.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">surfing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> For a <a href = vnd.unilang:surfboard.html>surfboard</a> to stand upright half-submerged in the water (like a <a href = vnd.unilang:tombstone.html>tombstone</a>, above) because the surfer <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> underwater with his or her legrope pulled tight. Often this indicates a surfer in difficulty, either <a href = vnd.unilang:held.html>held</a> down by the power of a wave or unconscious and unable to get to the surface.
<ul><li><b>2005</b>, Bruce Jenkins, <i>Surfer</i> magazine, (referring to <a href = vnd.unilang:kelly.html>Kelly</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:slater.html>Slater</a>) <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://surfermag.com/features/events/mav05/">[1]</a>:
<dl><dd>Before the contest <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> started, <a href = vnd.unilang:slater.html>Slater</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:went.html>went</a> down hard in a warmup session. He <a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> a two-wave hold-down in the semifinals, his board <b>tombstoning</b> eerily for all to see, <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> computing<span class="ib-comma">,</span> Microsoft <a href = vnd.unilang:windows.html>Windows</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To replace (an object or data) with a <a href = vnd.unilang:tombstone.html>tombstone</a> marker.
<ul><li><b>2000</b>, William Boswell, <i>Inside <a href = vnd.unilang:windows.html>Windows</a> 2000 Server</i> (page 211)
<dl><dd>One of the many improvements in <a href = vnd.unilang:windows.html>Windows</a> 2000 WINS (and NT4 SP4) <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the capability to selectively delete or <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tombstone.html>tombstone</a></b> records.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tomen.html>tomen</a> (58933)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tômen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tōmen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*taumijan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*taumijaną</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toom.html>toom</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">briddle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toneel-.html>toneel-</a></h1><br>theatrical</br></body> 
***toneel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toneel.html>toneel</a> (3935)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tineel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">tinel</i>; further origin uncertain. The modern Dutch term <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> adapted to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tonen.html>tonen</a></i> by folk etymology.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toneel.html>toneel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toneel.html>tonelen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toneel.html>toneeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>stage, scene, place for a performance in front of an assembled audience</li>
<li>scene, depiction on stage <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">often in the diminutive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> or part of a performance</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">used absolutely, with definite article: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toneel.html>toneel</a></i></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">theatre</span>, the dramatical <a href = vnd.unilang:arts.html>arts</a>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:theater.html>theater</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> theatre, <span class="Latn" lang="en">site</span> where something (a crime, battle...) <a href = vnd.unilang:happens.html>happens</a>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:theater.html>theater</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">stage</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:podium.html>podium</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:planken.html>planken</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">scene</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">scene</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">tableau-vivant</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:toneel.html>toneel</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>
